57   private def messageDigest: MessageDigest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256")

59   def run(limit: Option[Int],
60           submittedQueryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], List[QuerySolution]] = {
61     val queryGraph = enforceQueryEdgeTypes(submittedQueryGraph)
62     val nodeTypes = getNodeTypes(queryGraph.nodes)
63     for {
64       predicates <- ZIO.foreachPar(queryGraph.edges.filter(edge => edge._2.predicate.nonEmpty)) { (k, v) =>
65         for {
66           foundPredicates <- getTRAPIQEdgePredicates(v)
67           predicates = foundPredicates.map(a => sparql" $a ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
68           edgeIDVar = Var(k)
69           edgeSourceVar = Var(v.subject)
70           edgeTargetVar = Var(v.`object`)
71           sparqlChunk =
72             sparql"""
73                  VALUES $edgeIDVar { $predicates }
74                  $edgeSourceVar $edgeIDVar $edgeTargetVar .
75               """
76         } yield (v, sparqlChunk)
77       }
78       (edges, sparqlLines) = predicates.unzip
79       nodesToDirectTypes = getNodesToDirectTypes(queryGraph.nodes)
80       projections = getProjections(queryGraph)
81       moreLines = for {
82         id <- edges.flatMap(a => List(a.subject, a.`object`))
83         subjVar = Var(id)
84         v <- nodeTypes.get(id)
85       } yield sparql"$subjVar $RDFType $v ."
86       valuesClause = (sparqlLines ++ moreLines).fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
87       limitSparql = getLimit(limit)
88       queryString = sparql"""
89                           SELECT DISTINCT $projections
90                           WHERE {
91                             $nodesToDirectTypes
92                             $valuesClause
93                           }
94                           $limitSparql
95                           """
96       response <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQuery(queryString.toQuery)
97     } yield response
98   }
99 
100   def parseResultSet(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
101                      querySolutions: List[QuerySolution]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], TRAPIMessage] =
102     for {
103       biolinkData <- biolinkData
104       initialKGNodes <- getTRAPINodes(queryGraph, querySolutions)
105       initialKGEdges <- getTRAPIEdges(queryGraph, querySolutions)
106       querySolutionsToEdgeBindings <- getTRAPIEdgeBindingsMany(queryGraph, querySolutions)
107       trapiBindings <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
108         getTRAPINodeBindings(queryGraph, querySolution) zip Task.effect(querySolutionsToEdgeBindings(querySolution))
109       }
110       allEdgeBindings = trapiBindings.flatMap(_._2).toMap
111       allCamIds = allEdgeBindings.values.flatten.filter(a => a.provenance.isDefined).map(a => a.provenance.get)
112       prov2CAMStuffTripleMap <- ZIO.foreachPar(allCamIds)(prov => getCAMStuff(IRI(prov)).map(prov -> _)).map(_.toMap)
113       allCAMTriples = prov2CAMStuffTripleMap.values.to(Set).flatten
114       allTripleNodes = allCAMTriples.flatMap(t => Set(t.subj, t.obj))
115       slotStuffNodeDetails <- getTRAPINodeDetails(allTripleNodes.to(List), biolinkData.classes)
116       extraKGNodes = getExtraKGNodes(allTripleNodes, slotStuffNodeDetails, biolinkData)
117       allPredicates = allCAMTriples.map(_.pred)
118       slotStuffList <- getSlotStuff(allPredicates.to(List))
119       extraKGEdges = allCAMTriples.flatMap { triple =>
120         for {
121           slotStuff <- slotStuffList.find(_.kid == triple.pred)
122           predBLTermOpt = biolinkData.predicates.find(a => a.iri == slotStuff.biolinkSlot)
123         } yield getTRAPIEdgeKey(predBLTermOpt, triple.subj.value, triple.obj.value) -> TRAPIEdge(triple.subj,
124                                                                                                  triple.obj,
125                                                                                                  None,
126                                                                                                  predBLTermOpt,
127                                                                                                  None)
128       }.toMap
129 
130       results = trapiBindings.map { case (resultNodeBindings, resultEdgeBindings) => TRAPIResult(resultNodeBindings, resultEdgeBindings) }
131       finalResults = results
132       trapiKGNodes = initialKGNodes ++ extraKGNodes
133       trapiKGEdges = initialKGEdges ++ extraKGEdges
134 
135     } yield TRAPIMessage(Some(queryGraph), Some(TRAPIKnowledgeGraph(trapiKGNodes, trapiKGEdges)), Some(finalResults.distinct))
136 
137   def getNodeTypes(nodes: Map[String, TRAPIQueryNode]): Map[String, IRI] =
138     nodes
139       .map(entry =>
140         (entry._2.category, entry._2.id) match {
141           case (_, Some(c))    => List(entry._1 -> c)
142           case (Some(t), None) => List(entry._1 -> t.iri)
143           case (None, None)    => Nil
144         })
145       .flatten
146       .toMap
147 
148   def getNodesToDirectTypes(nodes: Map[String, TRAPIQueryNode]) =
149     nodes
150       .map { node =>
151         val nodeVar = Var(node._1)
152         val nodeTypeVar = Var(s"${node._1}_type")
153         sparql""" $nodeVar $SesameDirectType $nodeTypeVar .  """
154       }
155       .fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
156 
157   def getLimit(limit: Option[Int]) = {
158     val limitValue = limit.getOrElse(1000)
159     if (limitValue > 0) sparql" LIMIT $limitValue" else sparql""
160   }
161 
162   def getProjections(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph) = {
163     val projectionVariableNames =
164       queryGraph.edges.flatMap(entry => List(entry._1)) ++ queryGraph.edges.flatMap(e => List(e._2.subject, e._2.`object`)) ++ queryGraph.nodes.map(entry =>
165         s"${entry._1}_type")
166     projectionVariableNames.map(Var(_)).map(v => sparql" $v ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
167   }
168 
169   def enforceQueryEdgeTypes(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): TRAPIQueryGraph = {
170     val improvedEdgeMap = queryGraph.edges.map { case (edgeID, edge) =>
171       val newPredicate = edge.predicate match {
172         case None          => Some(BiolinkPredicate("related_to"))
173         case somePredicate => somePredicate
174       }
175       edgeID -> edge.copy(predicate = newPredicate)
176     }
177     queryGraph.copy(edges = improvedEdgeMap)
178   }
179 
180   def getTRAPIEdgeKey(pred: Option[BiolinkPredicate], sub: String, obj: String) = {
181     val edgeKey = TRAPIEdgeKey(pred, sub, obj).asJson.deepDropNullValues.noSpaces
182     String.format("%064x", new BigInteger(1, messageDigest.digest(edgeKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))))
183   }
184 
185   def getTRAPIEdges(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
186                     querySolutions: List[QuerySolution]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Map[String, TRAPIEdge]] =
187     for {
188       trapiEdges <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
189         for {
190           nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(entry => (entry._1, IRI(querySolution.getResource(s"${entry._1}_type").getURI))))
191           edges <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.edges) { (k, v) =>
192             for {
193               source <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(v.subject)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get source id"))
194               target <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(v.`object`)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get target id"))
195             } yield getTRAPIEdgeKey(v.predicate, v.subject, v.`object`) -> TRAPIEdge(source, target, None, v.predicate, None)
196           }
197         } yield edges.toList
198       }
199     } yield trapiEdges.flatten.toMap
200 
201   def getTRAPINodes(
202     queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
203     querySolutions: List[QuerySolution]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], Map[IRI, TRAPINode]] = {
204     val allOntClassIRIsZ = ZIO
205       .foreach(querySolutions) { qs =>
206         ZIO.foreach(qs.varNames.asScala.filter(_.endsWith("_type")).to(Iterable)) { typeVar =>
207           ZIO.effect(IRI(qs.getResource(typeVar).getURI)).mapError { e =>
208             new Exception(s"Value of _type variable $typeVar is not a URI", e)
209           }
210         }
211       }
212       .map(_.flatten)
213     for {
214       allOntClassIRIs <- allOntClassIRIsZ
215       biolinkData <- biolinkData
216       nodeDetails <- getTRAPINodeDetails(allOntClassIRIs, biolinkData.classes)
217       termToLabelAndTypes = nodeDetails.groupBy(_.term).map { case (term, termsAndTypes) =>
218         val (labels, biolinkTypes) = termsAndTypes.map(t => t.label -> t.biolinkType).unzip
219         term -> (labels.flatten.headOption, biolinkTypes)
220       }
221       trapiNodes <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
222         for {
223           nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(entry => (entry._1, querySolution.get(s"${entry._1}_type").toString)))
224           nodes <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.nodes) { (k, v) =>
225             for {
226               nodeIRI <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(k)).orElseFail(new Exception(s"Missing node IRI: $k"))
227               labelAndTypes = termToLabelAndTypes.getOrElse(IRI(nodeIRI), (None, List(BiolinkNamedThing)))
228               (labelOpt, biolinkTypes) = labelAndTypes
229               biolinkTypesSet = biolinkTypes.to(Set)
230               nodeBiolinkTypes = biolinkData.classes.filter(c => biolinkTypesSet(c.iri))
231             } yield IRI(nodeIRI) -> TRAPINode(labelOpt, Some(nodeBiolinkTypes), None)
232           }
233         } yield nodes.toList
234       }
235     } yield trapiNodes.flatten.toMap
236   }
237 
238   def getTRAPINodeDetailsQueryText(nodeIdList: List[IRI], biolinkClasses: List[BiolinkClass]) = for {
239     // requiring biolinkType makes some terms not be found when these results are used elsewhere - must be handled there
240     namedThingBiolinkClass <- ZIO
241       .fromOption(biolinkClasses.find(a => a.shorthand == "named_thing"))
242       .orElseFail(new Exception("Could not find BiolinkClass:NamedThing"))
243     nodeIds = nodeIdList.map(n => sparql" $n ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
244     query <- Task.effect(
245       sparql"""SELECT ?term ?biolinkType (MIN(?term_label) AS ?label)
246          WHERE {
247            VALUES ?term { $nodeIds }
248            ?term $RDFSSubClassOf ?biolinkType .
249            ?biolinkType $BiolinkMLIsA* ${namedThingBiolinkClass.iri} .
250            OPTIONAL { ?term $RDFSLabel ?term_label }
251          }
252          GROUP BY ?term ?biolinkType"""
253     )
254   } yield query
255 
256   def getTRAPINodeDetails(nodeIdList: List[IRI],
257                           biolinkClasses: List[BiolinkClass]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType]] =
258     for {
259       queryText <- getTRAPINodeDetailsQueryText(nodeIdList, biolinkClasses)
260       termsAndBiolinkTypes <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType](queryText.toQuery)
261     } yield termsAndBiolinkTypes

263   def getTRAPINodeBindings(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
264                            querySolution: QuerySolution): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig], Map[String, List[TRAPINodeBinding]]] =
265     for {
266       nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(n => (n._1, querySolution.get(s"${n._1}_type").toString)))
267       nodeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.nodes) { (k, v) =>
268         for {
269           nodeIRI <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(k)).orElseFail(new Exception(s"Missing node IRI: $k"))
270         } yield k -> List(TRAPINodeBinding(IRI(nodeIRI)))
271       }
272     } yield nodeBindings
273 
274   def getTRAPIEdgeBindingsMany(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph, querySolutions: List[QuerySolution])
275     : ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], Throwable, Map[QuerySolution, Map[String, List[TRAPIEdgeBinding]]]] = {
276     val solutionTriples = for {
277       queryEdge <- queryGraph.edges
278       solution <- querySolutions
279     } yield Triple(
280       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge._2.subject).getURI),
281       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge._1).getURI),
282       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge._2.`object`).getURI)
283     )
284     for {
285       provs <- getProvenance(solutionTriples.to(Set))
286       querySolutionsToEdgeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
287         for {
288           edgeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.edges) { (k, v) =>
289             for {
290               predicateRDFNode <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(k).toString)
291               sourceRDFNode <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(v.subject).toString)
292               targetRDFNode <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(v.`object`).toString)
293               edgeKey = getTRAPIEdgeKey(v.predicate, sourceRDFNode, targetRDFNode)
294             } yield k -> List(TRAPIEdgeBinding(edgeKey, provs.get(TripleString(sourceRDFNode, predicateRDFNode, targetRDFNode))))
295           }
296         } yield querySolution -> edgeBindings
297       }
298     } yield querySolutionsToEdgeBindings.toMap
299   }
300 
301   def getProvenanceQueryText(edges: Set[Triple]) = {
302     val values = edges.map(e => sparql"( ${e.subj} ${e.pred} ${e.obj} )").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
303     Task.effect(
304       sparql"""SELECT ?s ?p ?o ?g ?other
305         WHERE {
306           VALUES (?s ?p ?o) { $values }
307           GRAPH ?g { ?s ?p ?o }
308           OPTIONAL { ?g $ProvWasDerivedFrom ?other . }
309         }"""
310     )
311   }
312 
313   def getProvenance(edges: Set[Triple]): ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Throwable, Map[TripleString, String]] =
314     for {
315       queryText <- getProvenanceQueryText(edges)
316       querySolutions <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQuery(queryText.toQuery)
317       triplesToGraphs <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { solution =>
318         Task.effect {
319           val graph = if (solution.contains("other")) solution.getResource("other").getURI else solution.getResource("g").getURI
320           val triple = TripleString(solution.getResource("s").getURI, solution.getResource("p").getURI, solution.getResource("o").getURI)
321           triple -> graph
322         }
323       }
324     } yield triplesToGraphs.toMap
325 
326   def getCAMStuffQueryText(prov: IRI) = Task.effect(
327     sparql"""SELECT DISTINCT (?s_type AS ?subj) (?p AS ?pred) (?o_type AS ?obj)
328          WHERE { GRAPH $prov {
329              ?s ?p ?o .
330              ?s $RDFType $OWLNamedIndividual .
331              ?o $RDFType $OWLNamedIndividual .
332            }
333          ?o $SesameDirectType ?o_type .
334          ?s $SesameDirectType ?s_type .
335          FILTER(isIRI(?o_type))
336          FILTER(isIRI(?s_type))
337        }"""
338   )
339 
340   def getCAMStuff(prov: IRI): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[Triple]] =
341     for {
342       queryText <- getCAMStuffQueryText(prov)
343       triples <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[Triple](queryText.toQuery)
344     } yield triples

346   def getExtraKGNodes(camNodes: Set[IRI],
347                       slotStuffNodeDetails: List[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType],
348                       biolinkData: BiolinkData): Map[IRI, TRAPINode] = {
349     val termToLabelAndTypes = slotStuffNodeDetails.groupBy(_.term).map { case (term, termsAndTypes) =>
350       val (labels, biolinkTypes) = termsAndTypes.map(t => t.label -> t.biolinkType).unzip
351       term -> (labels.flatten.headOption, biolinkTypes)
352     }
353     val nodeMap = camNodes.map { node =>
354       val (labelOpt, biolinkTypes) = termToLabelAndTypes.getOrElse(node, (None, List(BiolinkNamedThing)))
355       val biolinkTypesSet = biolinkTypes.to(Set)
356       val classes = biolinkData.classes.filter(c => biolinkTypesSet(c.iri))
357       node -> TRAPINode(labelOpt, Some(classes), None)
358     }.toMap
359     nodeMap
360   }
361 
362   def getSlotStuffQueryText(predicates: List[IRI]) = {
363     val values = predicates.zipWithIndex
364       .map { case (p, i) =>
365         val id = StringUtils.leftPad(i.toString, 4, '0')
366         val qid = s"e$id"
367         sparql" ( $p $qid ) "
368       }
369       .fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
370     Task.effect(
371       sparql"""SELECT DISTINCT ?qid ?kid ?biolinkSlot ?label
372          WHERE {
373            VALUES (?kid ?qid) { $values }
374            ?kid $SlotMapping ?biolinkSlot .
375            ?biolinkSlot a $BiolinkMLSlotDefinition .
376            OPTIONAL { ?kid $RDFSLabel ?label . }
377            FILTER NOT EXISTS {
378              ?kid $SlotMapping ?other .
379              ?other $BiolinkMLIsA+/<https://w3id.org/biolink/biolinkml/meta/mixins>* ?biolinkSlot .
380            }
381          }"""
382     )
383   }
384 
385   def getSlotStuff(predicates: List[IRI]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[SlotStuff]] = for {
386     queryText <- getSlotStuffQueryText(predicates)
387     results <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[SlotStuff](queryText.toQuery)
388   } yield results
389 
390   def getTRAPIQEdgePredicatesQueryText(edgeType: IRI) = Task.effect(
391     sparql"""SELECT DISTINCT ?predicate
392       WHERE {
393         ?predicate $SlotMapping ${edgeType} .
394       }"""
395   )
396 
397   def getTRAPIQEdgePredicates(edge: TRAPIQueryEdge): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[IRI]] =
398     for {
399       edgeType <- ZIO.fromOption(edge.predicate).orElseFail(new Exception("failed to get edge type"))
400       queryText <- getTRAPIQEdgePredicatesQueryText(edgeType.iri)
401       predicates <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[Predicate](queryText.toQuery)
402     } yield predicates.map(_.predicate)
